msg:This is the fourth time I have stayed in this hotel. Every time I come to Hainan, I will stay here for three or four days. The cost-effectiveness is very high. You can stay in the hotel and swim to relax without going out. The hotel has various plants, and the most important thing is the water system. It is highly recommended for a family to live in the villa area.
Hygiene: Good.
Environment: Various tropical plants, the villa area is surrounded by water systems, there are mountains in the distance, and there is a lake at the entrance, which is tropical and beautiful. There is a food city nearby, and the hotel battery car can go there. The commercial street in the central area of ‚Äã‚ÄãYalong Bay is also very close.
Service: The cleaning lady and the battery car driver have a good attitude, and the front desk also introduces various things very clearly. The breakfast is more Chinese and the elderly may prefer it. If you have just moved from other international five-star hotels, there may be a gap. It belongs to the standard level of domestic five-star hotels. Free afternoon tea was given, some French fries, fruits, coffee, and Chinese steamed snacks for afternoon tea. People usually eat breakfast late. Having some afternoon tea at two or three o'clock can basically save a lunch. You need to take a battery car to go to the beach, which runs every half an hour and takes a few minutes to drive there.
Facilities: The hotel is indeed a bit old, and old things do exist, but the hotel still made some efforts, such as there is no socket at the head of the bed, the hotel pulled the magic cube plug board to the head of the bed. It is recommended to replace some of the broken soft furnishings, after all, some broken curtains are not very beautiful. However, basically, the price-performance ratio is high for staying in a villa with a swimming pool for the price of a night in a nearby international five-star sea view room. The defects are within an acceptable range. Finally, it is recommended that the hotel can buy some with a lower chassis when replacing the battery car in the future. At the current height, it is not friendly to the elderly with poor legs and feet.
